Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes upon its feet, it must be pushed upward.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn the buttocks from side to side until they are even.
puis preigne .i. des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then take one foot and extend it outward.   \]\]
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	It cannot jump up as high as the hips, if it is commanded to leap, and makes it vomit with discomfort.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If it jumps far, let it be.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not jump as much as we said, if you turn it little by little until it is according to the natural shape.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it becomes easy.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons dit, si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en .i. mortier;	And if it does not come out as we have said, take muscle salve of high quality, olive oil, melted resin, and grind everything in one mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement,	and apply the mixture onto the female side (of the body) and turn it outward (towards the affected area);
puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	then make her sit in hot water up to below the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai .i. coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	And when it becomes soft within, make one myrrh collar and place it under, and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then make it sit on a seat, then make it vomit and hold its mouth and nose tightly, and press gently on the stomach as the child jumps now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the child's birth upon its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this form, place the midwife's hands on it here and there;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor .i. lit;	Then let it hang from its neck, and its legs dangle downwards, and let it lie on one bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	And fold its hands palm to palm, and then press the hands on its stomach, and open the bladder under them, until it is exposed below.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	And if the infant does not breathe, take its legs and bend them, then move its stomach upward, then insert your hands.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc; et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	And rock the child little by little; and instruct the woman that she should take care until the birth of the baby.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	The birth of the child is coming out one hand's breadth wide.
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary to find a way to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	If you cannot bring it back, make her stand up and walk.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus .i. lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If it cannot walk, make it lie down on a bed, spread its legs apart.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then bring the mustard plaster as I have mentioned;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she is not in labor, make her sit on a chair, then study how to reposition the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and deliver the child according to its natural form, make it vomit, and order it to grip tightly as long as the afterbirth comes out;
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	The issue of the child on its neck, and he has spread his hands, and his face turned towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary that you hold his hand, then turn it little by little, and pull it gently.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is even, you should place natural muscle relaxant ointment of high quality and oil on it, as we have said, then you should instruct her to move it little by little.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.	and when you have done this, make her sit on a chair, and tell her to grasp herself, and make her vomit.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In this same manner, all must be reduced.
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes to reduce in this manner, grasp the reduction with your nail until the moisture is voided.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the limb presses upon its face and neck, grasp it by the root so that it is not held back, and kill the limb.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	Then push the child inside as far as you need to, so that it is positioned correctly, and instruct the woman to take herself once:
adonques si istra legierement.	then gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the birth of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent .iij. ou .iiij.; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	Know that twins are often born, and sometimes three or four; and it is not strange, and it happens often.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	These are strange things, and do not live unless named;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they multiply, and are distressed by the one who designs them, who is tied to the devil;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they come out naturally like a tooth, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if it discharges loudly, the treatment should be as we have said, and the balm should be subtle, and make it quickly and lightly as it does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and make it as it is worth moving towards healing.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris .i. ou .ij. ou .iij. ou .iiij. ou .v. ou .vj. ou .vij., ou plusors jusc’a .xv., et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious,	At no time are they formed in marriage. I.e., 1, 2, 3, or 4, or 5, or 6, or 7, or more up to 15, and all are formed in the shape of a child according to the measurement of the sacred manhood.
et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	And it is necessary that the bailiff knows all this, for by chance similar things may happen;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	follow what is necessary according to this.
de l’enfant mort	of a dead child.
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you are treating the woman with a dead child or pregnancy and it does not come out, and you are forced to perform manual labor;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	it is necessary for you to know whether the woman is of good health, and does not have any accident or fear of death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	the woman must lie on her back, with her head inclined downwards and legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de .ij. pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the attendant shall bind her loins with two bands, or tie her to the bed so she cannot be treated in delivering the child.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then anoint the husband's mouth with oil mixed with musk and fennel seeds, then anoint his hands with these oils and these musks.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere .i. leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu,	Then push it gently into the socket, then seek one side or the other where it can be pushed in.
et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	and take care if the bones are splintered on top of his head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez,	if you stick the bones back in their place or neck, mouth, throat, under the beard, wrist or near the sides,
et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	And if the dislocation is on limbs, pierce or press it gently with fingers.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	Then place the thumb of your right hand on the dislocation and put the back of your left hand between them, and push it gently with all your left hand, and insert the thumb into one of the places we have mentioned until it comes to an empty state.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the shape of the thumb:
puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then insert it against another thumb or the third one if necessary, so that the extraction is even.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then it should be straightened equally by moving it from one side to another, so that it may come out, and the joints should be grinded down to hold, as shown in the figure:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	If any part remains, then oil some of his fingers with oil and push it into that part, and pull the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if there remains no part at all, then place this instrument higher up and continue until it comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes in front of the other, and it cannot be returned due to strain.
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	you must roll up a cloth over it until it stops.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	then apply the splint at the joint of the palm or the wrist, and in this way you should do for the other hand and the feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the child's hips are large and he is narrow at the outlet, or has a sharp head assembled,   .......
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	It is necessary for you to push the sharp spathulum between your teeth, and bend it and draw out the pus.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	You grind the instrument called "almidach" to shape it with the tools or chapter that follows it.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and similarly, you treat a hernia naturally with a strong blow.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	And then extract the bones with the tongs,
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	If the joint jumps out and it is held by the forceps, it should be cut, as far as the moisture that is farther out goes.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	If it cannot come out, hit it in parts with what you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it swells in the belly or beneath the ribs, then you must pierce it until the moisture subsides.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on his feet, its removal will be easy and redirecting it to the mouth of the wound will be easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is narrow in the belly or the loins, then you must draw it out with one folded cloth on your hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and pierce the belly or the loins until the moisture subsides.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	And if the other member is dislocated, and the head remains,   (translation)
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	Push the ball in deep into the wound of the bladder, and pull it until it reaches the mouth of the bladder;   (translation)
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	Then put one or two fingers inside and pull out;   (translation)
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	And if the mouth of the bladder is narrowed by a hot abscess that has come in, there is no need to work on it;   (translation)
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	It is necessary to administer moist and fat substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	And apply ointments, soften and moisten them in warm water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	If the inflammation is on the costal side (ribcage), and you can equalize it, apply what has been said in the previous line.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	If there is no possibility of repairing it, cut it into pieces and leave nothing of the second part.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, bring it to him as we have said in the treatment of abscesses, those that come in marriage;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding comes out, it should be stopped by cautery, and bring other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whom the child inside was dead, then consulted another on this and revived the child.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came in the groin, and swelled so much that it opened, and began to putrefy greatly.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the healing, and for a long time I considered it, but could not stop the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I placed strong adhesive plaster on it, and after some days another bone appeared.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled greatly, since the stomach has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	I probe (or examine) the wound, and insert my hand bones as far as the woman's condition allows.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And keep the woman in this position for a long time, and at that point apply a little more traction on the bone.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have not heard of this chapter being used except for when the master finds an unusual problem that he knows how to help with it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to put the arm back in its place (or socket)
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Here comes the first sentence to translate:
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	The horns should be more delicate than the restrainer, and made of ebony or boxwood.
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And the mouth of the tube should be one finger wide, and the margins of the wood pieces one finger thick, and one and a half palm long.
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And in the two limbs should be two similar joints of the same bone, which are closed on both sides, half a palm long or slightly more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	And these two joints are pushed into the mouth of the mortar to open when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made of ivory or beechwood, similar to pliers;
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	And say to the two shoulders, as you see, of one span in length, and two fingers in width;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you see to open the woman with all the instruments, make her sit on one bed, her feet hanging down and legs apart;
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	Then push the two shoulders together inside the woman, and hold the head of the instrument beneath between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand with all the instruments, as you have done with the pliers equally, according to the quantity that you see to open the mouth of the anvil, until the bail makes it do what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These tools are all covered and have similar appearances; and when the blacksmith has equipped them, they work more quickly, and higher for humans because of their size.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Never disdain the tool that you have not equipped, for its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second child is retained during birth, it is necessary to command the patient to hold back her milk, and then make her vomit with emetics, and hold her hands at the mouth and anus.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she jumps because of that, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If that does not happen, take a pot and make a plaster or cover and put herbs inside that can open the mouth of the woman, such as rue, anise, chamomile, camphor, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked or boiled in water over fire; then put a cloth or lid on the pot, and pour the other end into the mouth of the patient.
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	And let the steam go inside the patient's mouth until the vapors come within, then make him vomit, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the patient suddenly jumps up.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	If it remains after this treatment and does not heal, as commanded to the woman, let her moisten her left hand with oil of thyme or musk oil of alum, and then apply it to the natural openings.
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And seek the second joint; and when you have found it, grasp it gently and extend it little by little straightway, so that the muscles do not resist extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	but you must move it gently to the right and left, and then pull; if it comes out and dislocates again.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the opening of the muscle is stretched, we have said the remedy for evacuation and fumigation with herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	And if it [the dislocation] is not all of what we have said, be careful when pulling [it].
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	But it is necessary that the one at the mouth of the bladder [urethra], tie it to the woman's leg, then cleanse it with a fourfold ointment.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	If she [the woman] passes it and replaces it again, and comes to pass feces; however, in any case, if it emits a bad smell from the stomach and head, burn the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	Therefore, it is necessary to use suitable fumigations for this condition; no one of the ancients has tested fumigation with dill and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman for retaining the flowers and the afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And is shaped like glass similar to a cane, with the tip thin in its nature and wide at the end over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigation be above the coals, and hold it until it is burned out, then start another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce through the bottom
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the bottom pierced, but it has been stopped by a subtle obstruction.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, it is necessary to pierce the obstruction at its right place with a suitable instrument and not with a sharp splinter, and ensure that it does not touch the child.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then put warm linen soaked in wine and oil on top of it and treat with ointment until healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will reopen, place a plank on it and leave it for many hours, and it should be taken off when the child wishes to go to bed.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes this sudden swelling of a wound or abscess occurs; it must be covered: whether treated, as we have said, with the poultice of lead.
de la fistule dou fondement	Of the fistula from the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from below the foundation are nodular, and larger than those that come out of it divert, or in the space between the two parts,
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	If there is a fistula or several; and when that swelling becomes old, it bursts, and moisture causes a wound to appear white or subtle pus.
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And sometimes these fistulas are persistent; and they are recognized by those who have them or exudation or wind when the patient evacuates, and possibly by a sudden jump in one direction.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if there are fistulas that extend to the bladder and halfway up the penis; they reach the knee joint and the ankle.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes the fistula persistent at the base, and not at the surface:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you press your thumb or index finger at the base, and insert a thin awl of iron or steel into the fistula where there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	if it has twisting, then insert a thin splint of wood or horse hair until you feel the splint or hair at your thumb:
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no pus, gas, or worm, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	Know that it does not pierce at all; hasten to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And if the fistula extends to the bladder or leads to the flow of urine, if it gushes forth, and cannot be sealed with medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced to the juncture of the thigh, then the tendon comes out at the level;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no twisting or the onset of pain around it, then it will remain bowed and no medicine nor salve can help it.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these Persian blisters there is no cure except labor, and vain attempts of foolish physicians who interfere.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In those not Persian and not ancient, with hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced,
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And it is that the patient lies between your hands on his back; and he raises his legs up to his thighs, and has his thighs inclined towards his belly.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then insert a tent of arrows or wood if there is a curve, until you know where the tent comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the patient feels it around the foundation, then it is necessary that you insert your finger as an indicator,
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	then it is known that the tent has pierced through; and whether it has pierced through the bone or flesh, in this case you will know that it is a hernia.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If one does not work on it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One should always understand that some can be healed well, but this happens seldom;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that one does, if it is heating the cautery gently according to the width of the wound, as was said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	And push everything hot into the fistula until it comes out from the base; and do this twice or thrice, as long as you know that these charred objects should be burned, which are similar to a feather of an eye.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	Then, heal the swollen swelling with moistened cloths, until the charred objects issue forth; then heal it with ointment that burns and cements.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it is thus healed, that is good. If this, however, cannot be healed;   In this context, "ensi" means "thus", "sanez" means "healed", and "ceu" refers to the condition or injury being treated. The phrase "nom autrement ne puet estre sanez" can be translated as "if it cannot be healed in any other way".
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if it tries to enter [the wound], and does not pierce to the correct depth which is the foundation, and put between your thumb and the tent a thick cover of flesh or leather, and you see the fistula at that place where the cover is cut.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the tip of the fistula's beginning touches the tent and it presses forward against the tent, and then apply the cautery after, until it reaches the top of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	The tent will be relieved and it will burst; then cut off the fatty tissues that seem like a bird's feather, and do not leave anything behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the bone pierces through [the flesh], and cuts into you or the work, then cauterize it with fire or medicine ointment.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For the fire cautery has two effects: namely, burning of charred joints and stopping of blood and removal of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then the wound of wet tents is cured with butter or ground cheez until the flesh swells and the charred joints are burned in it.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound of the onions soaked in hard charcoal, and the medicines are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	When it is restored, it becomes healed and will not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes up to the full depth of its foundation and is removed from the body, push it in with your thumb or foundation, and investigate it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the opening and go in 2 fingers or the syringe or charms where it is about to pierce, but there is no other way of hope or promise except through the administration of one of the 3 methods:   (This seems to be missing a line)
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you strike it to the bottom, or if you can do so, you put plasters and treat it as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, lest you strike the holding member that supports the foundation, and the escape happens through it voluntarily.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	possibly it will heal, or you remove that covering and clean it after it is struck away from the foundation, whether by force or by another instrument.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then fashion that iron implement which is in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	Then study to heal the wound, and to stop the fistula on the side of its base; it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes fistulas are like this: and it is when you press the tent into the fistula, and it is where the base touches the skin above.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	Take a pierced tent with this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And insert one twisted thread into two, and insert the sheath along the whole thread into the fistula until it reaches its end.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is perforated on the edge of the base within, then extract the thread from that pierced area, so you push your finger or base.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	pull out the head of the thread, and bring the two shoulders together, and tighten one against the other, and leave it for one day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and hold it without moving until the pus that is between them boils and bursts;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it heals and becomes healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula is not pierced, then pierce it in any way possible, as long as it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it should not be covered too deeply and then treated until it heals as we have said.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of a spurlike spinous one from which they make a fistula is very sharp at both ends;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other hand not, because it should not be struck where it should not be struck, as you see here:
des emorroydes	hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are of two kinds: either they are inside the foundation, like a grain of resin, and there are small and large ones, and in the court nearby there is blood;
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	And if there is one or more (of them), and they are dislocated at the base and at the head of the base; but those that are dislocated have little moisture,
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	And furthermore, there is also sometimes a small amount of clear citron juice or blood, and they have the color of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have it within the base, is that you command the patient to strain to urinate in chambers, until the base subsides, and this appears in the urine;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If it is urgent, then you can cut it with scissors or hold it with your nail and crush it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the bones cannot be held by their moisture, take hold of it with a cloth or cotton, or a piece of linen;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	Then pull it straight, then strike it, and sprinkle some hot powders on it instead of cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you can cauterize as said in the chapter of cautery, then treat it with other remedies until it heals;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	if the foundation does not come out, then you should clisterize the patient with a biting and sharp clisterium to wash the affected area until it comes out easily.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patient can present themselves, and if their veins are forced from the foundation, this is an easy cure.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and it is that you grab them with your fingernail or tweezers, strike them, then cure them as we have said, until they are healthy, and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	It is necessary to apply the stitching in this manner: take one thread, put it on a needle, then pull the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and twist the two ends of the thread below the needle.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is wide, stretch the thread firmly, then knot the thread, and draw out the needle, and do this with all the others, leaving one for bleeding excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place a damp cloth soaked in rose oil or turpentine on the foundation, and command the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then leave it until it stops bleeding, and when it has stopped, cure it with salve and other treatments until it is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	of the fire or foundation   (This line seems to be incomplete or missing some part)
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is drying of the intestines due to fire and by natural constriction, and when the disease is old and the medicine has no effect.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary for you to scrape with a splint or your nail the bark above, which prevents it from becoming wet.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	and then heal it until it heals as required;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot heal, then begin the shaving more strongly than before, until it heals well, and scrape it.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then heal it until it is healed.
dou fremit	The trembling (or shivering)
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Louse is a small insect that burrows into the body and goes deep;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes it freezes (affects) the throat and one feels it as if dying from trembling, spreading throughout the body but more in the hands than other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the remedy is that you take a cane made of an ostrich feather or a strong goose feather, and place it on the trembling, encircling it completely with the red ring (of the cane);
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand all along the neck until you grasp everything around the swelling, and put it in place, and straighten the swelling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, do as with a dog or iron chain of this shape, and be subtle inside and pull it out from above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not pierce, for fear of the thumb; and press it hard. If you see, then cauterize the swelling, as described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	Of the form of the plaster
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes plasters of silver or arsenic, or melted beeswax or lard, are made; and sometimes such small and large instruments are made according to those for whom they are prepared.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, when administering to children or weak and suffering individuals, the plasters should be small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the small and large plasters is as follows: wide or flat, with the belly tied in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	And there should be an incision where the belly is tied, as you see, and the head should be pierced within; and on one side there should be two holes, and in the other one.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	And fill the belly or place medications from an animal bladder or parchment, and pierce it all around with small holes.
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and there should be one space between each hole, then insert into these holes one strong thread of twisted thread in 10 or more around it, and tie the belly together like a goatskin.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And when the medicine is within, if it is tied with a strong thread to the instrument in front, then plasterize; and this is the shape of a circle.
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and smear the head with a plaster of oil or egg yolk, or similar thing, then gently press it in.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the ministers squeeze it with their two hands together until it is all visible, then remove the plaster, and make the patient spread out his legs before you.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	If the medicine comes out, press as much as possible; and if it stays for an entire night, it is more effective aid.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you apply a plaster for the disease of stomach decay, and the medicine is hastened to heal, then continue it until it becomes healthy.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are based or an abscess, then apply the plaster as thin as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the subtle plaster when the skin is tightened:
des plaies	wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already said in the division the treatment of wounds; now we will tell you the treatments for hands and medicines, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and of how they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by thrust of a spear, cut with a sword and knife, or lance or fist or arrow, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	What is done according to the body's laws, such as wounds that fall on the neck, or on the head, or the chest, or the belly, or the liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	I will tell you the cure for each wound, and I will begin with simple wounds of the head, because memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	and when a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, take care if it is caused by an arrow or similar things, and the skin is torn completely and the wound is large;
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	And you have doubts when opening the abscess hot: if it makes a wound in the head itself, even if there comes little blood from the wound, and the wound is healing contrary to the damaged part.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And you should evacuate the patient's repletion of thick wine and meat.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	If it does not heal, let his meat be reduced, and do not let him drink wine, nor eat flesh.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And put on the wound, if hot abscess comes, cotton dampened in rose oil or in vinegar steeped.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no abscess hot, place on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood, and it is not moved by air or powder, I will say a little after;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the arrow has moved it, place on some unguents until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	If the wound is large like that of a sword and similar, and the lips cannot be closed with stitches, then join them by suturing, as I will say for abdominal wounds, by suture.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed of bone and gaping and does not stay closed, press it; then treat the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Instruct the patient to eat large meats such as cooked heads (testes), wheat, peas, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find or notice pus-covered skin without reaching the bone, press it all and pour boiling water over it, then treat it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	and if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which without cautery cannot be stopped, you should tie it with a thread if you find it dislocated.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	and if that doesn't help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, the cure is easy; it is that you put this powder which solidifies as soon as the flesh has healed.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the method of the powder is as follows: take incense one part; dragon's blood 2 parts; quicklime 4 parts and grind finely.    Et si tu ne pouvez pas en prendre .ij. parties de sanc de dragon, si pren les parties de sanc de serpent; ou il est malsain de prendre sanc de serpent, et pren une partie de gumme de cynnamome; mais on doit prendre gumme de cinnamome pour li cure les plaies qui sont en la teste.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	And apply the wound, hold it open-formed, until it drains well and unites with all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Then bind it up well, let it heal by itself if it does not swell; for the medicine is not removed until it has healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes this is done with chalk only, when there is no incense or dragon's blood, but the wound has not healed.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	If the wound has healed, do not put this powder on it in summer.    Et s’il est de hiemes, et s’il li soit froid, mets la poudre sur la plaie et l’oncist et le liens.  Et si il est chauwainz et le temps est doux, ne mets pas la poudre sur la plaie;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but place over some digested herbs, or pulps made of barley flour boiled with water and honey, until it flows out.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then heal it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the bone breaks along with the wound, and it is small, draw it out with fine forceps.
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	And I will tell you after the breaks of the head.
de la plaie dou col	Of the wound of the neck.
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If a wound comes or it is in the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between it and that of the head, but if the nerves of the neck or the artery are cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerves, there is no other remedy than to let them heal and not to put anything binding, because it hurts the nerves and makes them retreat;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And put nothing cold on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold, and the continuation of them is with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but let the medicine be warm, such as warm water washed in sweet oil, and cooked again in warm water.
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	And other stones of similar manner, and always moist.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound is large, cut it and bind it with bands, until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and she is swollen and full of pus, pierce it or lower the level.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	If the artery is cut and bleeding occurs, stop it, ligate it, and cauterize if necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	If the spine of the throat is cut or the trachea is damaged, keep it guarded so that the flesh can pass.
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	Cut the trachea above the throat and do not touch the throat but put it back in its natural position.
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then the straining comes, and it is left for some days, then it is cured with rejected ointments until it heals.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound presses against the bone, squeeze it;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are fragments of bone, pull them out completely if possible; and those that cannot be pulled out, leave until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	make the opening and align the edges;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, sprinkle on it the powder I have said.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and there is a fistula, treat it as I have said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound from spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a wound from spear or knife, and the wound is deep, look to see if the patient bleeds from the wound: know then that the wound is fatal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not fully healed and it is fresh with all its blood, do not put the powder on it at first hour nor bind it because the blood might dissolve it completely,
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	return to the heart, and cut open the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply atractive ointment and bind it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you don't have ointment, put old cotton in the wound to absorb moisture;
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	And make the patient sleep on the wound for three or four days, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	If no convulsions, nor bad tremors of heart, or any agony of the entrails come,
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see good signs, know that the wound is saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat the patient with tenting and other treatments, as long as he is healthy.
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	And if it cannot heal, and there is an opening, then make sure there is a fistula; treat it as needed.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife cut, and it is simple, or worse, or at the back, treat the one in front of it.
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it is large, stitch it; if it is small, powder it, and if it has penetrated the bone and split it, then treat the wound and pull out the foreign objects if they are loose.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they are not drained (or opened), let the wound fester, align the extractions.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	As for other wounds on other limbs, the judgement is similar as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	The rupture of the stomach (or abdomen)
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The rupture of the stomach can be great, medium, and small.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a large wound, the intestines may jump out occasionally, or parts of the intestines, due to this, insertion occurs.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and stitching is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worse than a large one.
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because then the intestines are inserted with greater difficulty if not inserted from end to end.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines expand when they feel pressure, so they go in more easily.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And because it is more beneficial for wounds to move, therefore one moves the intestines back to their place more than other two [parts].
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	Know that the hernia of the belly is according to four kinds:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The first two common hernias occur in the abdominal wall,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	And the stitching of other wounds on the body, and 2 additional stitches specific to these wounds, are common for other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	Moreover, they are more suitable with the stitching of the stomach, and I will tell one and explain each one:
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and nothing from the intestines protrudes,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	And a great thing is to reset, this is by one of the two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or through the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are inflamed due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, heat it in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	Moisten a sponge or a thin cloth in cold water only.
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	and you cook in hot squiant and cypress and spike.
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and pull out the intestines when the swelling has been removed;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes make this wine restraining, and it is mixed with sulphur to reduce swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling separate, if you moisten the intestines of aqueous or bad and ill-cooked [substances],
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for this way is narrow the entrance to something.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, then make a small incision in the instrument with which one strikes the hemorrhoids.
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first cure is to grind the tail (of the intestine).
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	We should not cut it except in great necessity.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument to split it:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut inside the hump and do not turn it, and look at its shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	When the wound is enlarged, and the intestines burst out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	If you reset it according to its natural shape in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	then, if possible, for it is necessary.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide and in the lower part of the belly,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you should make the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	And he should raise his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	If it is in the lower abdomen area,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	lift the head and the buttocks higher than the parts below;
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and if the rupture of the belly is in one of the two areas,
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	If the part (limb) is broken, it should be higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus you must treat as I say in large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	In small wounds, use what is appropriate (equipped).
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then have between your hands a compassionate minister who anoints the entire wound with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	and press your lips together;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common way of stitching,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you take a needle or more depending on the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	Then leave from the head of the wound, that is, a space of a thumb's width, and insert an awl or a strong threaded needle there.
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce the two hide layers with the two shoemaker's awls,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is beneath the skin inside, as long as you are piercing that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	And assemble the two heads of the sheep four together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then bind with a double thread around the needle of two parts (of the sheep),
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then assemble the two heads of the wound facing each other;
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	And then leave one finger's space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread in the same way as you did with the first needle.
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue to do so according to what you need with the needles.
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until the entire wound is held tight;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	And the needles shall be moderate, neither too thin nor thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	for fine needles pierce all the skin and large ones cannot enter well.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	therefore, they should be moderate.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and needles should not be pressed too far into the skin and flesh,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	"So they do not open and wound the wound before the suture."
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	"Then sew up the head of the arrows so that they do not pierce the patient while sleeping,"
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	"and bind cloth or patches to the head of the arrow to hold it in place,"
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	"and leave them until the wound is healed."
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	And this method of stitching with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it pierces an awl or two [through the wound].
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second type of stitching is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and it is that you assemble the two sides of the skin and the two sides of the flesh together with one awl having a strong medium thread.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	And when you have pierced these four things altogether,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	draw the needle back to the part where you started, in the manner that is customary with threads;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and place a space between each stitch of about the thickness of a thumbnail;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitching is for the man.
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	And I sew a wound that someone had or belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which was pierced with a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than one palm in length,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and it extended the intestines by two palms in length,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	And the wound was inside the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned the intestines after it had been twenty-four hours.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound was sewn up for fifteen days, and he recovered, and became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, and it was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	And do not treat it with ointment, for I am in one place where none can be found, nor any medicine.
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and put cotton wool twice a day on the wound, and wash it with water of honey until it is healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you the two proper ways of stitching:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and push it from the outside to the inside up until:
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	When it has pierced the heart straight through, if the chest is opened or costal cartilage cut where you inserted the needle,
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and cause it to be pierced from the inside part up until that point;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the understanding of this suture is that you sew as a tailor sews fur.
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and leave the chest open from one side and take it up from the other until the suture is complete.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of stitching, which Galen specifically calls,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	is such that they join the two parts together naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and apply one of its [the suture's] heads to the other, in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	Insert a needle or the next awl into that place alone, and pierce only that spot,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	And let the two shoulders rest.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	Then turn the needle and make it pass from the outer part to the inner one.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	until the two shoulders are at rest.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pass a needle through one and the other from the outer part to the inner one, in two other shoulders on the opposite side of the ribs.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the common method of stitching.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen said this word, and no one denies it.
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One should sew the stomach with two needles, each having thread in them;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one needle should be driven in from one side, and the other from the other, like those who sew leather.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	And know that when the hernia is inside the abdomen,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	is the stitching more painful than other places in the abdomen.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgement of the wound is such as the judgement of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and when you probe the fresh wound with all its blood, just as the arrow has moved it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	If one sets right the intestines, and the stitch; then put on top the powder stimulating flesh,
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if it has been moved, set some ointment that is available, until the wound heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and sew the flesh, and bind the seams, and the stitching;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then heal the wound as others, until it is healed;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	And if you do not have medicine, immediately place on top, as soon as it starts to throw out pus, old cotton.
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And move it two times a day until it is healthy.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you do not need other medicine in many situations when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound may affect the main members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	It is necessary that you soften linen lightly in warm oil or rose oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the swellings, and beneath the saddlebags;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if there is pain or pus in the belly, and it frequently happens,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if the clysterization with black wine is hot, and especially if pus comes all the way to the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And pierce it within, and know that when it is the large intestines, it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine called "jen" cannot heal when it is punctured.
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it is because of the inflammation of the veins that they are in, and due to the subtlety of the entire body, and the proximity of its nature to the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the worm jumps out from the wound, put it back in the same way as the intestine, while it is still fresh.
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it is old and turned or black, you must tie the blackened place so that blood does not flow from there.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	For there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	Then cut that which is between the ligament.
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	And place the two heads hanging from the part below the wound to straighten the extraction when the arrow falls, and the wound bows.
de la routure dou boueil	of the rupture of the bladder
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are torn, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	If it can be restored in some men,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I have seen that a man was wounded or pierced with a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and became an abscess and became a fistula, and in it was evacuation and flatulence;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I will treat him according to what I know, and I will not stop refining it until he is healthy again, and the limbs will be united.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I see them united, I fear that the patient may have something wrong in his stomach;
